## Dependencies

| Dependency | Classification | Reason |
|---|---|---|
| `async-trait` | neutral-rust-helper | trait object ergonomics for explicit runtime service contracts |
| `basalt` | yellow-dynamic-runtime-policy-data | policy/value representation for runtime orchestration receipts |
| `blake3` | neutral-receipt-hashing | deterministic hashes for runtime receipts and evidence |
| `chrono` | yellow-runtime-clock-dto | runtime/session DTO timestamps stay outside generic green SDK crates |
| `clanker-message` | green-sdk-data-contract | shared content and semantic-event contracts |
| `clankers-artifacts` | yellow-artifact-runtime-contract | runtime execution receipts and artifact DTOs |
| `clankers-engine` | green-sdk-engine-contract | engine message/model DTOs consumed through runtime adapters |
| `clankers-engine-host` | green-sdk-host-contract | host-owned engine execution seams used by runtime session shell |
| `clankers-tool-host` | green-sdk-tool-contract | neutral tool execution and capability contracts |
| `serde` | neutral-serialization | public DTO serialization |
| `serde_json` | neutral-serialization | receipt and metadata JSON values |
| `thiserror` | neutral-error-helper | typed RuntimeError display |
| `tokio` | yellow-runtime-async-shell | runtime/session async channels and explicit host service execution |
| `uuid` | yellow-runtime-identity-dto | runtime prompt/session identifiers stay app-edge |
